No database migration needed.', 'UserFacing': True}, 'CodeContent': '# Challan Tracking in Client Portal\n\n## Overview\n\nCurrently the Client Portal (`/portal`) only shows **Invoices** and **Ledger**. The client (party) has no visibility into their **Party Challans** (work orders received from them) or **Delivery Challans** (dispatched materials back to them). This feature adds a dedicated **Challans** section to the client portal so clients can self-track their order status in real-time.\n\n---\n\n## What the Client Sees\n\n### Party Challan Tracking\nA **Party Challan** represents material received **from** the client for processing.\n- Challan Number, Date, Status (`open` / `partial` / `completed` / `cancelled`)\n- Items: Item Name, Process, Qty Ordered, Qty Delivered so far (progress bar)\n- Linked Delivery Challans (what has been dispatched back)\n\n### Delivery Challan Tracking\nA **Delivery Challan** represents dispatched goods sent **back to** the client.\n- Challan Number, Date, Vehicle Number, Status (`draft` / `sent` / `delivered`)\n- Items: Item Name, Qty Sent, OK Qty, Rejected Qty (cr_qty), Rework Qty (mr_qty)\n- Download button for PDF (optional phase 2)\n\n---\n\n## Architecture — What Changes Where\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  CLIENT BROWSER  (/portal/challans)                     │\n│  ClientChallans.jsx  (NEW page)                         │\n│  Two tabs: Party Challans | Delivery Challans           │\n└────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘\n                         │  GET /client/party-challans\n                         │  GET /client/delivery-challans\n                         ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  BACKEND  client_portal.py  (MODIFY)                    │\n│  New endpoints — secured by get_current_client()        │\n│  Filters by client.party_id  (no cross-tenant leakage)  │\n└────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘\n                         │\n              ┌──────────┴──────────┐\n              ▼                     ▼\n        party_challan          delivery_challan\n        party_challan_items    delivery_challan_items\n        (existing tables — no schema migration needed)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Open Questions\n\n> [!IMPORTANT]\n> **Q1 – Delivery Challan PDF download in portal?**\n> Should clients be able to download Delivery Challan PDFs from their portal, just like Invoices? (This needs an extra endpoint and template rendering. I\'ll skip it in Phase 1 unless you say yes.)\n\n> [!IMPORTANT]\n> **Q2 – Show "cancelled" challans to client?**\n> Should clients see challans with `status = cancelled`? Recommended: hide them (same as invoices). Let me know if you want a toggle.\n\n> [!IMPORTANT]\n> **Q3 – Financial Year filter?**\n> The dashboard has a financial year dropdown. Should the Challans page also have this filter? (Recommended: yes, for consistency.)\n\n---\n\n## Proposed Changes\n\n### Backend — `client_portal.py`\n\n#### [MODIFY] [client_portal.py](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/backend/app/routers/client_portal.py)\n\nAdd two new endpoint groups at the bottom of the file:\n\n**1. `GET /client/party-challans`**\n- Auth: `get_current_client()` — only returns challans where `party_id == client.party_id`\n- Optional query param: `financial_year_id`, `status`\n- Returns: challan header + items (with item name, process name, qty_ordered, qty_delivered, progress %)\n- Excludes `cancelled` by default (configurable)\n\n**2. `GET /client/delivery-challans`**\n- Auth: `get_current_client()`\n- Optional: `financial_year_id`, `party_challan_id` (drill-down)\n- Returns: challan header + items (qty, ok_qty, cr_qty, mr_qty)\n- Also accepts `party_challan_id` to show only delivery challans for a specific party challan\n\n---\n\n### Frontend\n\n#### [NEW] Challans** | Table/card list of Delivery Challans with status badge and item quality breakdown |\n| **Detail Expand** | Click a challan row → expand to show all its items inline |\n\nStatus badges:\n- `open` → 🟡 Yellow\n- `partial` → 🔵 Blue\n- `completed` → 🟢 Green\n- `cancelled` → 🔴 Red (hidden by default)\n- `draft` → 🔘 Gray\n- `sent` → 🔵 Blue\n- `delivered` → 🟢 Green\n\nProgress bar for party challans:\n```\nItem: Steel Rod   [██████████░░░░░░░░░░] 50/100 kg (50%)\n```\n\n#### [MODIFY] [App.jsx](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/frontend/src/App.jsx)\n\nAdd route --- PIECE 1 ---
## Challan Tracking in Client Portal — My Analysis & Plan

Here's what I found in your codebase and what I'm recommending:

---

### Current Client Portal (`/portal`) Has:
| Route | Feature |
|---|---|
| `/portal/dashboard` | Stats, invoices chart |
| `/portal/invoices` | Invoice list + PDF download |
| `/portal/ledger` | Account ledger |
| `/portal/settings` | Profile + password |

**Missing: Zero visibility into Party Challans or Delivery Challans!**

---

### My Recommendation — Add `/portal/challans` Page

Based on your data models, here's how it works:

**Party Challan** = material the client sends **to you** for processing  
**Delivery Challan** = goods you send **back to** the client

So a client should see:
1. **"What I sent you"** → Party Challans (with progress bar: how much has been processed/returned)
2. **"What you sent back to me"** → Delivery Challans (with quality breakdown: OK qty / rejected / rework)

---

### What Needs to Be Built

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| [`client_portal.py`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/backend/app/routers/client_portal.py) | **+2 new endpoints** — `GET /client/party-challans` and `GET /client/delivery-challans` |
| `ClientChallans.jsx` | **New page** — two-tab UI with status badges, progress bars, item detail expansion |
| [`App.jsx`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/frontend/src/App.jsx) | Add `/portal/challans` route |
| `ClientLayout.jsx` | Add "Challans" nav link |

**No database changes needed** — all data is already in existing tables.

---

I've created the detailed implementation plan above. Please review and answer the 3 open questions, then click **Proceed** to start building!

{'ArtifactMetadata': {'RequestFeedback': False, 'Summary': 'New client portal page for tracking Party Challans and Delivery Challans. Features two tabs, financial year filter, status filter, cancelled toggle, progress bars, quality breakdown, and PDF download.', 'UserFacing': False}, 'CodeContent': 'import { useEffect, useState } from "react";\nimport { useClientAuth } from "../../context/ClientAuthContext";\nimport {\n  Package,\n  Truck,\n  ChevronDown,\n  ChevronUp,\n  Download,\n  Loader2,\n  Calendar,\n  Search,\n  Filter,\n  X,\n  CheckCircle,\n  Clock,\n  AlertCircle,\n  XCircle,\n  Eye,\n  RefreshCw,\n} from "lucide-react";\nimport toast from "react-hot-toast";\n\n// ─── Status Badge ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nconst STATUS_CONFIG = {\n  // Party Challan statuses\n  open: { label: "Open", color: "bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 dark:bg-yellow-900/30 dark:text-yellow-400", icon: Clock },\n  partial: { label: "Partial", color: "bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-400", icon: AlertCircle },\n  completed: { label: "Completed", color: "bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900/30 dark:text-green-400", icon: CheckCircle },\n  cancelled: { label: "Cancelled", color: "bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900/30 dark:text-red-400", icon: XCircle },\n  // Delivery Challan statuses\n  draft: { label: "Draft", color: "bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 dark:bg-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300", icon: Clock },\n  sent: { label: "Sent", color: "bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-400", icon: Truck },\n  delivered: { label: "Delivered", color: "bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900/30 dark:text-green-400", icon: CheckCircle },\n};\n\nfunction StatusBadge({ status }) {\n  const config = STATUS_CONFIG[status?.toLowerCase()] || STATUS_CONFIG.draft;\n  const Icon = config.icon;\n  return (\n    <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ${config.color}`}>\n      <Icon className="w-3 h-3" />\n      {config.label}\n    </span>\n  );\n}\n\n// ─── Progress Bar ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction ProgressBar({ percent, qty_ordered, qty_delivered }) {\n  const pct = Math.min(percent, 100);\n  const color =\n    pct >= 100 ? "bg-green-500" : pct >= 50 ? "bg-blue-500" : "bg-yellow-500";\n\n  return (\n    <div className="space-y-1">\n      <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">\n        <span>{qty_delivered} / {qty_ordered}</span>\n        <span className="font-semibold">{pct}%</span>\n      </div>\n      <div className="h-2 bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">\n        <div\n          className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500 ${color}`}\n          style={{ width: `${pct}%` }}\n        />\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n// ─── Financial Year Dropdown ──────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction FYDropdown({ financialYears, selected, onSelect }) {\n  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);\n  const label = selected\n    ? financialYears.find((fy) => fy.id === selected)?.year_name || "Selected"\n    : "All Years";\n\n  return (\n    <div className="relative">\n      <button\n        onClick={() => setOpen(!open)}\n        className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-sm hover:border-blue-400 dark:hover:border-blue-500 transition-all"\n      >\n        <Calendar className="w-4 h-4 text-blue-600" />\n        <span className="text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300">{label}</span>\n        <ChevronDown className={`w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 transition-transform ${open ? "rotate-180" : ""}`} />\n      </button>\n\n      {open && (\n        <div className="absolute left-0 top-full mt-1 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-xl z-20 min-w-[160px] overflow-hidden">\n          <button\n            onClick={() => { onSelect(""); setOpen(false); }}\n            className="w-full text-left px-4 py-2.5 text-sm hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300"\n          >\n            All Years\n          </button>\n          {financialYears.map((fy) => (\n            <button\n              key={fy.id}\n              onClick={() => { onSelect(fy.id); setOpen(false); }}\n              className={`w-full text-left px-4 py-2.5 text-sm hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700 ${selected === fy.id ? "text-blue-600 font-semibold" : "text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300"}`}\n            >\n              {fy.year_name} {fy.is_active && <span className="text-xs text-green-500">● Active</span>}\n            </button>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n// ─── Party Challan Card ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction PartyChallanCard({ challan }) {\n  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);\n\n  return (\n    <div className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 shadow-sm hover:shadow-md transition-all duration-200 overflow-hidden">\n      {/* Header */}\n      <div\n        className="flex items-center justify-between p-5 cursor-pointer group"\n        onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}\n      >\n        <div className="flex items-center gap-4">\n          <div className="p-2.5 bg-gradient-to-br from-violet-500 to-purple-600 rounded-xl shadow-sm">\n            <Package className="w-5 h-5 text-white" />\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">\n              <h3 className="font-bold text-gray-900 dark:text-white text-base">\n                {challan.challan_number}\n              </h3>\n              <StatusBadge status={challan.status} />\n            </div>\n            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 mt-0.5">\n              {new Date(challan.challan_date).toLocaleDateString("en-IN", {\n                day: "numeric", month: "short", year: "numeric"\n              })}\n              {challan.working_days && ` · ${challan.working_days} working days`}\n            </p>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">\n          <div className="text-right hidden sm:block">\n            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500">Dispatches</p>\n            <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200">\n              {challan.delivery_challan_count}\n            </p>\n          </div>\n          <div className="text-right hidden sm:block">\n            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500">Items</p>\n            <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200">\n              {challan.items.length}\n            </p>\n          </div>\n          <div className={`p-2 rounded-lg bg-gray-100 dark:bg-gray-700 text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 transition-transform duration-200 ${expanded ? "rotate-180" : ""}`}>\n            <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4" />\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Overall Progress Bar */}\n      {!expanded && challan.items.length > 0 && (() => {\n        const totalOrdered = challan.items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.quantity_ordered, 0);\n        const totalDelivered = challan.items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.quantity_delivered, 0);\n        const overallPct = totalOrdered > 0 ? Math.round(totalDelivered / totalOrdered * 100) : 0;\n        return (\n          <div className="px-5 pb-4">\n            <ProgressBar percent={overallPct} qty_ordered={totalOrdered} qty_delivered={totalDelivered} />\n          </div>\n        );\n      })()}\n\n      {/* Expanded Detail */}\n      {expanded && (\n        <div className="border-t border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-700 bg-gray-50/50 dark:bg-gray-900/30">\n          {challan.notes && (\n            <div className="px-5 py-3 bg-blue-50 dark:bg-blue-900/20 border-b border-blue-100 dark:border-blue-800/30">\n              <p className="text-xs text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-300">\n                <span className="font-semibold">Note:</span> {challan.notes}\n              </p>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          <div className="p-5 space-y-4">\n            <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500">\n              Item-wise Progress\n            </p>\n            {challan.items.map((item) => (\n              <div key={item.id} className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-xl p-4 border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">\n                <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">\n                  <div>\n                    <p className="font-semibold text-gray-900 dark:text-white text-sm">\n                      {item.item_name}\n                    </p>\n                    {item.process_name && (\n                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 mt-0.5">\n                        Process: {item.process_name}\n                      </p>\n                    )}\n                  </div>\n                  <span className="text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200 bg-gray-100 dark:bg-gray-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-lg">\n                    {item.progress_percent}%\n                  </span>\n                </div>\n                <ProgressBar\n                  percent={item.progress_percent}\n                  qty_ordered={item.quantity_ordered}\n                  qty_delivered={item.quantity_delivered}\n                />\n              </div>\n            ))}\n\n            {challan.items.length === 0 && (\n              <p className="text-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500 italic text-center py-4">\n                No items in this challan\n              </p>\n            )}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n// ─── Delivery Challan Card ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction DeliveryChallanCard({ challan, onDownload, downloadingId }) {\n  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);\n  const isDownloading = downloadingId === challan.id;\n\n  return (\n    <div className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 shadow-sm hover:shadow-md transition-all duration-200 overflow-hidden">\n      {/* Header */}\n      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-5">\n        <div\n          className="flex items-center gap-4 cursor-pointer flex-1"\n          onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}\n        >\n          <div className="p-2.5 bg-gradient-to-br from-teal-500 to-cyan-600 rounded-xl shadow-sm">\n            <Truck className="w-5 h-5 text-white" />\n          </div>\n          <div>\n            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">\n              <h3 className="font-bold text-gray-900 dark:text-white text-base">\n                {challan.challan_number}\n              </h3>\n              <StatusBadge status={challan.status} />\n            </div>\n            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 mt-0.5">\n              {new Date(challan.challan_date).toLocaleDateString("en-IN", {\n                day: "numeric", month: "short", year: "numeric"\n              })}\n              {challan.vehicle_number && ` · 🚛 ${challan.vehicle_number}`}\n              {challan.party_challan_number && (\n                <span className="ml-1 text-violet-600 dark:text-violet-400 font-medium">\n                  · Ref: {challan.party_challan_number}\n                </span>\n              )}\n            </p>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">\n          <button\n            onClick={() => onDownload(challan.id, challan.challan_number)}\n            disabled={isDownloading}\n            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-semibold text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-400 bg-blue-50 dark:bg-blue-900/20 hover:bg-blue-100 dark:hover:bg-blue-800/30 rounded-xl border border-blue-200 dark:border-blue-800 transition-all disabled:opacity-60"\n            title="Download PDF"\n          >\n            {isDownloading ? (\n              <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" />\n            ) : (\n              <Download className="w-4 h-4" />\n            )}\n            <span className="hidden sm:inline">PDF</span>\n          </button>\n          <button\n            onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}\n            className={`p-2 rounded-xl bg-gray-100 dark:bg-gray-700 text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 transition-transform duration-200 ${expanded ? "rotate-180" : ""}`}\n          >\n            <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4" />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Expanded Items */}\n      {expanded && (\n        <div className="border-t border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-700 bg-gray-50/50 dark:bg-gray-900/30">\n          {challan.notes && (\n            <div className="px-5 py-3 bg-teal-50 dark:bg-teal-900/20 border-b border-teal-100 dark:border-teal-800/30">\n              <p className="text-xs text-teal-700 dark:text-teal-300">\n                <span className="font-semibold">Note:</span> {challan.notes}\n              </p>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          <div className="p-5 space-y-3">\n            <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500">\n              Item Quality Breakdown\n            </p>\n\n            {challan.items.length === 0 ? (\n              <p className="text-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500 italic text-center py-4">\n                No items recorded\n              </p>\n            ) : (\n              <div className="overflow-x-auto">\n                <table className="w-full text-sm">\n                  <thead>\n                    <tr className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500 uppercase border-b border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-700">\n                      <th className="text-left pb-2">Item</th>\n                      <th className="text-left pb-2">Process</th>\n                      <th className="text-right pb-2">Qty</th>\n                      <th className="text-right pb-2 text-green-600">OK</th>\n                      <th className="text-right pb-2 text-red-500">Rej.</th>\n                      <th className="text-right pb-2 text-orange-500">Rework</th>\n                    </tr>\n                  </thead>\n                  <tbody className="divide-y divide-gray-50 dark:divide-gray-700/50">\n                    {challan.items.map((item) => (\n                      <tr key={item.id} className="group">\n                        <td className="py-2.5 pr-2 font-medium text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200">\n                          {item.item_name}\n                        </td>\n                        <td className="py-2.5 pr-2 text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 text-xs">\n                          {item.process_name || "—"}\n                        </td>\n                        <td className="py-2.5 text-right text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 font-medium">\n                          {item.quantity}\n                        </td>\n                        <td className="py-2.5 text-right font-semibold text-green-600">\n ## ✅ Challan Tracking Feature — Complete

### What Was Built

#### Backend — [`client_portal.py`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/backend/app/routers/client_portal.py)

Added **3 new secure endpoints**:

| Endpoint | Description |
|---|---|
| `GET /client/party-challans` | All party challans for the client — with per-item delivery progress |
| `GET /client/delivery-challans` | All delivery challans dispatched to the client — with quality breakdown |
| `GET /client/delivery-challans/{id}/download` | PDF download (same template as admin) |

All endpoints are secured by `get_current_client()` — a client can **only see their own challans**.

#### Frontend

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| [`ClientChallans.jsx`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/frontend/src/pages/client/ClientChallans.jsx) | ✅ New page (22KB) |
| [`App.jsx`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/frontend/src/App.jsx) | ✅ Added `/portal/challans` route |
| [`ClientLayout.jsx`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/frontend/src/layouts/ClientLayout.jsx) | ✅ Added 🚛 **Challans** nav link |

### Features in the UI

- **Two tabs** — Party Challans | Delivery Challans
- **Progress bar** for each party challan item (color: 🟡 <50% → 🔵 50%+ → 🟢 100%)
- **Quality breakdown table** for delivery challans: Qty / OK / Rejected / Rework
- **Status badges** with color coding (open, partial, completed, cancelled, sent, delivered)
- **Financial Year filter** (auto-selects active FY)
- **Status filter** dropdown
- **Cancelled toggle** (hide/show cancelled challans)
- **Search** by challan number
- **PDF download** button on every delivery challan
- Works on **mobile** (bottom nav tab) and **desktop** (sidebar)

Visit **`/portal/challans`** to see the new page in action!
--- PIECE 13 ---
Now I understand the full picture. The `generate_pdf` returns **HTML bytes**. The existing pattern is `media_type="text/html"` — the frontend handles printing via a hidden iframe + `window.print()`. The download button in `ClientChallans.jsx` is doing a raw `fetch → blob → anchor download`, which saves the HTML as a `.pdf` file — that's why the browser can't open it.

The fix is in the **frontend**: instead of downloading the blob as a file, **open the HTML response in a new tab** and let the browser print it (just like the existing invoice print pattern works).

Let me check how the existing invoice view/print works to match the pattern:
--- PIECE 14 ---
Now I see the full picture. The invoice `handleDownload` also does `blob → a.download` — meaning the invoice download has the **same bug** (downloads HTML as .pdf). The real working pattern must use a **new tab with `window.print()`**. Let me fix the `handleDownloadDC` function in `ClientChallans.jsx` to open the HTML in a new window and auto-print it:

All references are clean. The fix is complete. Here's the summary:

---

## Root Cause & Fix

### Why it Failed
The **`generate_pdf` service** in your backend ([`pdf_service.py`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/backend/app/services/pdf_service.py)) does **NOT generate actual PDF bytes**. It intentionally returns **raw HTML bytes** instead (WeasyPrint/Playwright were disabled for hosting compatibility). The comment in the file explicitly says:

> *"The frontend is responsible for triggering `window.print()` on this HTML."*

So when the old code did `blob → a.download = "DC-xxx.pdf"`, it saved an HTML file with a `.pdf` extension — which Chrome then refused to open as a PDF.

### What Was Fixed — [`ClientChallans.jsx`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/frontend/src/pages/client/ClientChallans.jsx)

| Before ❌ | After ✅ |
|---|---|
| `fetch → blob → a.download → .pdf file` | `fetch → res.text() → window.open() → window.print()` |
| Browser gets HTML but tries to open as PDF | Browser renders HTML and opens native Print dialog |
| "Failed to load PDF document" error | User sees rendered challan → can Print or **Save as PDF** |

The button was also renamed from **"Download PDF"** to **"View / Print"** with a 🖨️ Printer icon to correctly reflect the behavior. The user can use **Print → Save as PDF** in the browser dialog to get a proper PDF file.

--- PIECE 45 ---
Both backend and frontend are clean. Here's what was fixed:

---

## ✅ Party Challan Numbers Now Shown on Delivery Challan Cards

### Root Cause
DC-004 had `party_challan_id = NULL` (no direct link), so the old code `c.party_challan.challan_number if c.party_challan else None` returned nothing.

But the party challan **can still be found** through the items chain:
```
DeliveryChallanItem → party_challan_item → party_challan
```

### What Was Fixed

**Backend — [`client_portal.py`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/backend/app/routers/client_portal.py)**
- Changed `party_challan_number: str | None` → `party_challan_numbers: List[str]`
- Now collects from **both sources**:
  1. Direct `party_challan_id` FK (if set)
  2. Each item's `party_challan_item → party_challan` (always checked)
- Returns a **sorted, deduplicated list** — so if a DC covers multiple PCs, all show up

**Frontend — [`ClientChallans.jsx`](file:///d:/2026/SmartBill%20FastAPI/smartBILL/frontend/src/pages/client/ClientChallans.jsx)**
- Displays each party challan number as a **violet badge** inline with the challan date
- Search now works across all referenced PC numbers

**Result:** DC-004 will now show `PC-001` (or whatever the correct challan is) as a violet badge next to the date.

    - Fixed `ReferenceError: printingPcId is not defined`: Identified that the "Download Report" button was misplaced inside `DeliveryChallanCard` instead of `PartyChallanCard`. Removed the button from the wrong component.

### 4. Model Knowledge
- Architecture & Interfaces: 
    - `ClientChallans.jsx` contains both `PartyChallanCard` and `DeliveryChallanCard` components.
    - `ClientAuthContext.jsx` stores client info as `{ id, partyId, partyName }`.
- Constraints: The backend `login_access_token` returns `party_name`, but the token itself does not contain this field in the payload, requiring state management to handle the `partyName` correctly upon login.
- Failures: The `ReferenceError` occurred because `printingPcId` state is managed in the parent component and passed as props, but it was being accessed in a component that didn't have the prop defined or the state available.

32: function StatusBadge({ status }) {
33:   const config = STATUS_CONFIG[status?.toLowerCase()] || STATUS_CONFIG.draft;
34:   const Icon = config.icon;
35:   return (
36:     <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ${config.color}`}>

38:       {config.label}
39:     </span>
40:   );
41: }

43: function ProgressBar({ percent, qty_ordered, qty_delivered }) {
44:   const pct = Math.min(percent, 100);
45:   const color = pct >= 100 ? "bg-green-500" : pct >= 50 ? "bg-blue-500" : "bg-yellow-500";
46:   return (
47:     <div className="space-y-1">
48:       <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
49:         <span>{qty_delivered} / {qty_ordered}</span>
50:         <span className="font-semibold">{pct}%</span>
51:       </div>
52:       <div className="h-2 bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
53:         <div className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500 ${color}`} style={{ width: `${pct}%` }} />
54:       </div>
55:     </div>
56:   );
57: }

59: function FYDropdown({ financialYears, selected, onSelect }) {
60:   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);

62:   return (
63:     <div className="relative">
64:       <button onClick={() => setOpen(!open)} className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-sm hover:border-blue-400 dark:hover:border-blue-500 transition-all">
65:         <Calendar className="w-4 h-4 text-blue-600" />
66:         <span className="text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300">{label}</span>
67:         <ChevronDown className={`w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 transition-transform ${open ? "rotate-180" : ""}`} />
68:       </button>
69:       {open && (
70:         <div className="absolute left-0 top-full mt-1 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-xl z-20 min-w-[160px] overflow-hidden">

83: function PartyChallanCard({ challan, handlePrintPC, printingPcId }) {
84:   const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
85:   const totalOrdered = challan.items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.quantity_ordered, 0);
86:   const totalDelivered = challan.items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.quantity_delivered, 0);
87:   const overallPct = totalOrdered > 0 ? Math.round(totalDelivered / totalOrdered * 100) : 0;
88: 
89:   return (
90:     <div className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 shadow-sm hover:shadow-md transition-all duration-200 overflow-hidden">

32: function StatusBadge({ status }) {
33:   const config = STATUS_CONFIG[status?.toLowerCase()] || STATUS_CONFIG.draft;
34:   const Icon = config.icon;
35:   return (
36:     <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ${config.color}`}>

38:       {config.label}
39:     </span>
40:   );
41: }

43: function ProgressBar({ percent, qty_ordered, qty_delivered }) {
44:   const pct = Math.min(percent, 100);
45:   const color = pct >= 100 ? "bg-green-500" : pct >= 50 ? "bg-blue-500" : "bg-yellow-500";
46:   return (
47:     <div className="space-y-1">
48:       <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
49:         <span>{qty_delivered} / {qty_ordered}</span>
50:         <span className="font-semibold">{pct}%</span>
51:       </div>
52:       <div className="h-2 bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
53:         <div className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500 ${color}`} style={{ width: `${pct}%` }} />
54:       </div>
55:     </div>
56:   );
57: }

59: function FYDropdown({ financialYears, selected, onSelect }) {
60:   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
61:   const label = selected ? financialYears.find((fy) => fy.id === selected)?.year_name || "Selected" : "All Years";
62:   return (
63:     <div className="relative">
64:       <button onClick={() => setOpen(!open)} className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-sm hover:border-blue-400 dark:hover:border-blue-500 transition-all">
65:         <Calendar className="w-4 h-4 text-blue-600" />
66:         <span className="text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300">{label}</span>
67:         <ChevronDown className={`w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 transition-transform ${open ? "rotate-180" : ""}`} />
68:       </button>
69:       {open && (
70:         <div className="absolute left-0 top-full mt-1 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-xl z-20 min-w-[160px] overflow-hidden">
71:           <button onClick={() => { onSelect(""); setOpen(false); }} className="w-full text-left px-4 py-2.5 text-sm hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300">All Years</button>
72:           {financialYears.map((fy) => (
73:             <button key={fy.id} onClick={() => { onSelect(fy.id); setOpen(false); }} className={`w-full text-left px-4 py-2.5 text-sm hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700 ${selected === fy.id ? "text-blue-600 font-semibold" : "text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300"}`}>
74:               {fy.year_name} {fy.is_active && <span className="text-xs text-green-500">? Active</span>}
75:             </button>
76:           ))}
77:         </div>
78:       )}
79:     </div>
80:   );

287: function EmptyState({ icon: Icon, title, description, color = "blue" }) {
288:   const gradients = { violet: "from-violet-400 to-purple-500", teal: "from-teal-400 to-cyan-500", blue: "from-blue-400 to-indigo-500" };
289:   return (
290:     <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-20 gap-4 text-center">
291:       <div className={`p-5 bg-gradient-to-br ${gradients[color]} rounded-2xl shadow-lg opacity-30`}>
292:         <Icon className="w-10 h-10 text-white" />
293:       </div>
294:       <div>
295:         <p className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300">{title}</p>
296:         <p className="text-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500 mt-1 max-w-xs">{description}</p>
297:       </div>
298:     </div>
299:   );
300: }

302: export default function ClientChallans() {
303:   const { client } = useClientAuth();
304:   const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("party");
305:   const [partyChallans, setPartyChallans] = useState([]);
306:   const [deliveryChallans, setDeliveryChallans] = useState([]);
307:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
308:   const [financialYears, setFinancialYears] = useState([]);
309:   const [selectedFY, setSelectedFY] = useState("");
310:   const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState("");
311:   const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState("");
312:   const [includeCancelled, setIncludeCancelled] = useState(false);
313:   const [printingId, setPrintingId] = useState(null);
314:   const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState("");
315:   const [endDate, setEndDate] = useState("");
316:   const [printingPcId, setPrintingPcId] = useState(null);
317: 
318:   const token = localStorage.getItem("client_token");
319: 
320:   const fetchFY = async () => {
321:     try {
322:       const res = await fetch(`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/client/financial-years`, { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } });
323:       if (!res.ok) return;
324:       const data = await res.json();
325:       setFinancialYears(data);
326:       const active = data.find((fy) => fy.is_active);
327:       if (active) setSelectedFY(active.id);
328:     } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
329:   };
330: 
331:   const fetchPartyChallans = async () => {
332:     setLoading(true);
333:     try {
334:       let url = `${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/client/party-challans?include_cancelled=${includeCancelled}`;
335:       if (selectedFY) url += `&financial_year_id=${selectedFY}`;
336:       if (statusFilter) url += `&status=${statusFilter}`;
337:       if (startDate) url += `&start_date=${startDate}`;
338:       if (endDate) url += `&end_date=${endDate}`;
339:       const res = await fetch(url, { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } });
340:       if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Failed to load party challans");
341:       setPartyChallans(await res.json());
342:     } catch (e) { toast.error(e.message); } finally { setLoading(false); }
343:   };
344: 
345:   const fetchDeliveryChallans = async () => {
346:     setLoading(true);
347:     try {
348:       const params = [];
349:       if (selectedFY) params.push(`financial_year_id=${selectedFY}`);
350:       if (statusFilter) params.push(`status=${statusFilter}`);
351:       if (startDate) params.push(`start_date=${startDate}`);
352:       if (endDate) params.push(`end_date=${endDate}`);
353:       const url = `${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/client/delivery-challans${params.length ? "?" + params.join("&") : ""}`;
354:       const res = await fetch(url, { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } });
355:       if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Failed to load delivery challans");
356:       setDeliveryChallans(await res.json());
357:     } catch (e) { toast.error(e.message); } finally { setLoading(false); }
358:   };
359: 
360:   const handlePrintDC = async (challanId) => {
361:     setPrintingId(challanId);
362:     try {
363:       const res = await fetch(
364:         import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL + '/client/delivery-challans/' + challanId + '/download',
365:         { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + token } }
366:       );
367:       if (!res.ok) {
368:         const err = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
369:         throw new Error(err.detail || 'Failed to load challan');
370:       }
371:       const html = await res.text();
372:       const printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
373:       if (!printWindow) {
374:         toast.error('Popup blocked - please allow popups for this site');
375:         return;
376:       }
377:       printWindow.document.write(html);
378:       printWindow.document.close();
379:       printWindow.focus();
380:       setTimeout(function() { printWindow.print(); }, 800);
381:       toast.success('Challan opened - use Print > Save as PDF to download.');
382:     } catch (e) {
383:       toast.error(e.message);
384:     } finally {
385:       setPrintingId(null);
386:     }
387:   };
388: 
389:   useEffect(() => { fetchFY(); }, []);
390:   useEffect(() => {
391:     if (activeTab === "party") fetchPartyChallans();
392:     else fetchDeliveryChallans();
393:   }, [activeTab, selectedFY, statusFilter, includeCancelled, startDate, endDate]);
394: 
395:   const filteredParty = partyChallans.filter((c) => c.challan_number.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()));
396:   const filteredDelivery = deliveryChallans.filter((c) => c.challan_number.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) || (c.party_challan_numbers || []).some((n) => n.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase())));
397:   const statusOptions = activeTab === "party" ? ["open", "partial", "completed", "cancelled"] : ["draft", "sent", "delivered"];
398: 
399:   const handleExportCSV = () => {
400:     const list = activeTab === "party" ? filteredParty : filteredDelivery;
401:     if (!list.length) return toast.error("No data to export");
402: 
403:     let csv = "";
404:     if (activeTab === "party") {
405:       csv = "Challan Number,Date,Status,Total Ordered,Total Delivered,Progress %\n";
406:       list.forEach(c => {
407:         const ord = c.items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.quantity_ordered, 0);
408:         const del = c.items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.quantity_delivered, 0);
409:         const pct = ord > 0 ? Math.round((del/ord)*100) : 0;
410:         csv += `${c.challan_number},${c.challan_date},${c.status},${ord},${del},${pct}%\n`;
411:       });
412:     } else {
413:       csv = "Delivery Challan No,Date,Status,Vehicle No,Party Challan Refs\n";
414:       list.forEach(c => {
415:         const refs = c.party_challan_numbers ? c.party_challan_numbers.join("; ") : "";
416:         csv += `${c.challan_number},${c.challan_date},${c.status},${c.vehicle_number || ""},${refs}\n`;
417:       });
418:     }
419: 
420:     const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: "text/csv" });
421:     const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
422:     const a = document.createElement("a");
423:     a.href = url;
424:     a.download = `${activeTab}_challans_${new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0]}.csv`;
425:     document.body.appendChild(a);
426:     a.click();
427:     document.body.removeChild(a);
428:     window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
429:   };
430: 
431:   const handlePrintPC = async (challanId) => {
432:     setPrintingPcId(challanId);
433:     try {
434:       const res = await fetch(
435:         import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL + '/client/party-challans/' + challanId + '/report/download',
436:         { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + token } }
437:       );
438:       if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Failed to load report");
439:       const html = await res.text();
440:       const printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
441:       if (!printWindow) return toast.error('Popup blocked - please allow popups');
442:       printWindow.document.write(html);
443:       printWindow.document.close();
444:       printWindow.focus();
445:     } catch (e) { toast.error(e.message); } finally { setPrintingPcId(null); }
446:   };
447: 
448:   // Stats calculations for Dashboard
449:   const stats = {
450:     openPartyChallans: partyChallans.filter(c => c.status === "open" || c.status === "partial").length,
451:     pendingItems: partyChallans.filter(c => c.status === "open" || c.status === "partial").reduce((sum, c) => sum + c.items.reduce((s, i) => s + Math.max(0, i.quantity_ordered - i.quantity_delivered), 0), 0),
452:     totalDispatches: partyChallans.reduce((sum, c) => sum + c.delivery_challan_count, 0)
453:   };
454: 
455:   return (
456:     <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto space-y-6 pb-10">
457:       <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center sm:justify-between gap-4">
458:         <div>
459:           <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 dark:text-white flex items-center gap-3">
460:             <span className="p-2 bg-gradient-to-br from-violet-500 to-purple-600 rounded-xl">
461:               <Package className="w-6 h-6 text-white" />
462:             </span>
463:             Challans
464:           </h1>
465:           <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 mt-1 ml-12">Track your material orders and dispatches</p>

51:       </div>

340:       if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Failed to load party challans");
341:       setPartyChallans(await res.json());
342:     } catch (e) { toast.error(e.message); } finally { setLoading(false); }
343:   };

352:       if (endDate) params.push(`end_date=${endDate}`);

386:     }

43: function ProgressBar({ percent, qty_ordered, qty_delivered }) {
44:   const pct = Math.min(percent, 100);
45:   const color = pct >= 100 ? "bg-green-500" : pct >= 50 ? "bg-blue-500" : "bg-yellow-500";
46:   return (
47:     <div className="space-y-1">
48:       <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
49:         <span>{qty_delivered} / {qty_ordered}</span>
50:         <span className="font-semibold">{pct}%</span>
51:       </div>
52:       <div className="h-2 bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
53:         <div className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500 ${color}`} style={{ width: `${pct}%` }} />
54:       </div>
55:     </div>
56:   );
57: }
